The AOT source-contract suite now also locks generated value-frame cleanup: `backend_aot_c_frame_cleanup.*` must exist, generated C must include `zr_vm_core/function.h` and `zr_vm_core/type_layout.h`, `ZR_AOT_C_FAIL()` must route through `ZR_AOT_C_RETURN(...)` rather than directly returning, dispatch/default/return paths must use the shared exit, cleanup must emit `zr_aot_value_frame_drop` blocks with `ZrCore_TypeLayout_DropInline`, and typed inline return must set `zr_aot_skip_drop_slot` before `ZR_AOT_C_RETURN(1)`.

The same cleanup/failure source-contract test now also locks direct generated failure reporting. The RED check first failed on missing `ZrCore_Debug_RunError(state,` in `ZR_AOT_C_FAIL()`, then passed after the macro emitted the generated failure message, frame/instruction metadata, and `ZR_AOT_C_RETURN(0)`, while `backend_aot_c_function_body.c` zero-initialized `ZrAotGeneratedFrame frame = {0};`. The contract forbids `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_FailGeneratedFunction(state, &frame)` in checked generated-C emission.

The same source-contract target now also locks explicit unsupported generated-instruction boundaries. `test_aot_c_source_emits_value_frame_cleanup_exit` first failed on missing `backend_aot_write_c_unsupported_instruction(file,`, then passed after invalid branch targets, default opcode lowering paths, and fallthrough paths emitted `zr_aot_unsupported_instruction`, `unsupported AOT instruction`, `ZrCore_Debug_RunError`, and `ZR_AOT_C_FAIL()` instead of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ReportUnsupportedInstruction`.

The same source-contract target now also locks removal of typed function-body begin-instruction emission. The older RED/GREEN path first introduced a direct `zr_aot_begin_instruction` block to replace `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_BeginInstruction`; 07-S1 supersedes that shape for typed generated C by forbidding `backend_aot_write_c_begin_instruction(` in `backend_aot_c_function_body.c`. The focused generated-product test also rejects `zr_aot_begin_instruction`, preserving the 07 environment-isolation requirement while keeping the helper body available until the later MethodInfo/observation cleanup.

The same source-contract target now also locks direct generated pending-control lowering. The RED check first failed on missing `backend_aot_write_c_pending_control_transfer(FILE *file,`, then passed after `SET_PENDING_RETURN`, `SET_PENDING_BREAK`, and `SET_PENDING_CONTINUE` emitted direct pending-control blocks with `execution_set_pending_control`, `execution_resume_pending_via_outer_finally`, target jumps through `execution_jump_to_instruction_offset`, active-frame refresh, and generated dispatch. A production scan over `backend_aot_c*.c` found no C-backend `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SetPendingReturn`, `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SetPendingBreak`, or `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SetPendingContinue` emission.

The separate call source-contract target locks dynamic, generic, static, and meta-call boundary lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_quickened_dynamic_calls_to_direct_core_calls` first failed on missing `zr_aot_direct_dynamic_function_call`, and later failed on missing SemIR-aware dispatch when a source fixture produced a `DYN_TAIL_CALL` SemIR row on a generic call bytecode opcode. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_function_calls_to_direct_core_calls` first failed while `backend_aot_write_c_direct_function_call()` still emitted `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_PrepareDirectCall`, then passed after generic direct calls reused the stack-anchor/core-call template. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_static_direct_calls_to_direct_core_calls` first failed while static direct calls still emitted `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_PrepareStaticDirectCall` / `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_FinishDirectCall`, then passed after static resolved calls emitted `zr_aot_direct_static_function_call`, `ZrCore_Closure_GetMetadataFunctionFromValue`, staged call-window setup through `ZrCore_Function_GetCallInfoFrameStorageTop`, `ZrCore_Function_PreCallPreparedResolvedVmFunctionWithArgumentSource`, generated thunk invocation, and `ZrCore_Function_PostCall`. `test_aot_c_source_makes_meta_calls_explicit_boundary` first failed while meta-call bytecodes still used the old prepared-call helper pair, then passed after those bytecodes emitted `zr_aot_unsupported_meta_call` and an explicit unsupported boundary. The contract now requires SemIR-aware dynamic routing, generic direct call lowering, static `zr_aot_direct_static_function_call` lowering, stack anchors, `ZrCore_Function_CallAndRestoreAnchor`, destination anchor restore, direct result copy, staged resolved VM pre/post-call setup with argument-source frame metadata, frame refresh, explicit meta-call unsupported-boundary markers, absence of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_Call(state, &frame...)` from dynamic call lowering, absence of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_PrepareDirectCall` from generic direct-call lowering, absence of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_PrepareStaticDirectCall` / `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_FinishDirectCall` from static direct-call lowering, and absence of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_PrepareMetaCall` / `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallPreparedOrGeneric` from meta-call lowering. `tests/parser/test_aot_c_call_shared_library_smoke.c` compiles a generated C shared library for a source-level indirect call, verifies both static and dynamic direct-core call behavior in the generated C, executes it through the AOT runtime on Unix toolchains, separately executes a generated value-SemIR typed-call module to lock POD struct return C behavior, and separately compiles a hand-built meta-call fixture to lock the unsupported-boundary generated C surface without executing that intentional failure path.

The same suite now also locks the generated-module ABI surface: `zr_vm_common/include/zr_vm_common/zr_aot_abi.h` must exist in the real public include tree and expose the generated C descriptor/export types used by `backend_aot_c_emitter.c`. It also locks `SZrAotWriterOptions` and the AOT C/LLVM writer entrypoints in `writer.h`. Focused GCC/Clang syntax checks for `backend_aot_c_emitter.c`, frame cleanup, function body, value SemIR, and control lowering now use the normal public include paths without any local `SZrAotWriterOptions` typedef, so missing ABI or writer declarations no longer hide behind `.codex` verification fixtures.

`tests/parser/test_aot_c_source_contracts.c` now owns the archived AOT C source-contract assertions that were split out of `tests/parser/test_semir_pipeline.c`. The split keeps SemIR pipeline tests focused on compiler/runtime artifacts while giving AOT C lowering contracts their own growth boundary.

The AOT C source-contract suite now checks that typed scalar signed/unsigned/float arithmetic exposes dedicated emitter declarations, emits source-level C `+`, `-`, `*`, `/`, and unary `-zr_aot_source_scalar` expressions from `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_arithmetic.c`, routes the corresponding non-const typed arithmetic opcodes from `backend_aot_c_function_body.c`, and no longer prints direct `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_*` arithmetic helper calls for those opcode families. It also checks signed/unsigned const arithmetic emitter declarations, constant literal formatting, `zr_aot_left_scalar +|-|*|/ zr_aot_right_literal` source expressions, function-body routing for const typed arithmetic opcodes, direct `ADD_SIGNED_MOD_CONST` lowering with `(zr_aot_left_scalar + zr_aot_right_scalar) % zr_aot_mod_literal`, and absence of direct const arithmetic helper strings for those signed/unsigned opcode families.

The source-contract suite now also locks primitive constant direct writes. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_primitive_constants_to_direct_value_writes` first failed on the missing `backend_aot_write_c_direct_primitive_constant` emitter, then passed after `GET_CONSTANT` immediate primitive constants were routed to direct null/scalar writes and `SET_CONSTANT` was routed to direct constant-table assignment. The contract requires the generated source markers `zr_aot_value_exec_primitive_constant` and `zr_aot_value_exec_set_constant`, the direct `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET(zr_aot_destination, ...)` and `*zr_aot_constant = *zr_aot_source` shapes, and the absence of the old destination `ZrCore_Value_Copy(state, zr_aot_destination, &zr_aot_constant)` and generated-C `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SetConstant(state, &frame...)` paths. The hand-written ExecBC/AOT backend fixture now verifies the same C-side direct `SET_CONSTANT` shape while preserving the current LLVM expectation that still calls `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SetConstant`.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 signed constant first-read validation extended the typed scalar generated-product test. Signed primitive constants with i64 scalar-local coverage now emit a `zr_aot_scalar_constant_i64_local` assignment block before the current frame-write fallback, and the first i64 binary source path skips `frame.slotBase[0/1].value.type` checks when both operands are already written C locals. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. This is a partial 07-S2 step only: later primitive constant frame writes, scalar result frame writes, and other typed consumer frame checks remain open.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 signed bitwise source-local validation tightened the same typed scalar generated-product test. The old signed bitwise path for `zr_aot_s16 = zr_aot_s12 & zr_aot_s0` validated `frame.slotBase[12]` and `frame.slotBase[0]`, then reloaded both C locals from the frame before emitting the C `&` expression. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_i64_bitwise()` now checks `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_i64_written_before()` per source and skips frame validation/reload for already-written i64 locals, so the focused generated C keeps `zr_aot_s12` as the source of truth. The current proof is still block-local, so `slot 0` remains a conservative frame fallback in this fixture. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing; full 07-S2 remains open.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 signed shift source-local validation extended the same path to signed i64 shifts. The old shift lowering validated `frame.slotBase[15/16]` plus `frame.slotBase[1]`, then reloaded the left source and shift count before emitting `zr_aot_s19 = (TZrInt64)((TZrUInt64)zr_aot_s15 << zr_aot_s1)` or `zr_aot_s20 = zr_aot_s16 >> zr_aot_s1`. The signed shift emitter now applies the same per-source `i64_written_before` proof and keeps already-written left source locals in C; the shift count remains a frame fallback until cross-block source-local proofs cover `slot 1`. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 signed branch source-local validation removed another frame source dependency from typed scalar branch lowering. The first signed compare branch already emitted `if (zr_aot_s2 <= zr_aot_s4)`, but still built `SZrTypeValue` source pointers and checked `zr_aot_left->type` / `zr_aot_right->type` first. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_signed_branch()` now returns early with a pure C-local `if (zr_aot_s2 <= zr_aot_s4) { goto ...; }` block when both signed operands are proven written i64 locals. Constant signed branches and unproven cross-block cases still use the frame fallback. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 cross-block signed source-local validation widened the same proof from a block-local scan to conservative ExecIR must-write dataflow. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_i64_written_before()` now treats a C local as live at a block entry only when every reachable predecessor has written the same scalar kind, then still checks same-block prefix writes before the queried instruction. The focused typed scalar generated C no longer validates/reloads `frame.slotBase[2/3]` before the cross-block `zr_aot_s6 = zr_aot_s2 + zr_aot_s3` path, and constant signed branch lowering now emits `if (zr_aot_s2 != zr_aot_right_literal)` without a `SZrTypeValue` left source when the left slot is proven live. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. This is still partial 07-S2: destination frame writes and scalar result materialization remain.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 signed compare source-local validation applied the same per-source proof to scalar SemIR signed compare lowering. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_i64_compare()` now skips frame source checks and reloads for operands proven by `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_i64_written_before()`, so the focused generated C emits `zr_aot_b27 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_s2 > zr_aot_s4)` without first validating and reloading `frame.slotBase[2/4]`. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. The bool destination still uses the current frame-backed result materialization, so this remains partial 07-S2.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 signed conversion source-local validation applied the same written-before proof to signed-source numeric conversions. `backend_aot_try_write_c_scalar_conversion()` now passes the current exec instruction index into conversion emitters, allowing `TO_FLOAT_SIGNED` and `TO_UINT_SIGNED` to skip `frame.slotBase[2]` source assignment, source signed-type check, and reload when `zr_aot_s2` is proven written. The focused generated C keeps the direct casts `zr_aot_f31 = (TZrFloat64)zr_aot_s2` and `zr_aot_u31 = (TZrUInt64)zr_aot_s2`. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. Float-source and unsigned-source conversions still use frame-backed source reads until their written-before queries are exposed.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 unsigned source-local validation exposed the same must-write query for `u64` locals. Unsigned compare lowering, u64 bitwise binary lowering, and u64 bit-not lowering now skip source frame checks and reloads when `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_u64_written_before()` proves the source local is live. The focused generated C keeps `zr_aot_b14 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_u8 > zr_aot_u7)`, `zr_aot_b23 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_u21 <= zr_aot_u7)`, and `zr_aot_u33 = ~zr_aot_u7` without preceding source refreshes. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. Unsigned shift, unsigned/float conversions, float sources, destination frame writes, and result materialization remain open.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 unsigned conversion source-local validation then applied that `u64` proof to numeric conversions. `TO_FLOAT_UNSIGNED` and `TO_INT_UNSIGNED` now skip `frame.slotBase[8]` source assignment, source unsigned-type check, and reload when `zr_aot_u8` is proven written, while preserving the direct `(TZrFloat64)zr_aot_u8` cast and unsigned-to-signed wrap expression. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. Float-source conversion reads remain frame-backed until `f64` written-before queries are exposed.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 unsigned shift source-local validation completed the next u64 consumer slice. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_u64_shift()` now queries `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_u64_written_before()` for the left operand and `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_i64_written_before()` for the shift count, so the focused generated C keeps `zr_aot_u13 = zr_aot_u8 << zr_aot_s1` and `zr_aot_u14 = zr_aot_u10 >> zr_aot_s1` without source frame type checks or reloads when both sources are proven live. The shift-count range guard is preserved. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. Float sources, destination frame writes, and result materialization remain open for later 07-S2 slices.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 f64 source-local validation exposed the same written-before proof for float scalar locals. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_f64_binary()` now skips source frame type checks and reloads for `zr_aot_f19` / `zr_aot_f20` when both operands are proven written, while `TO_INT_FLOAT` and `TO_UINT_FLOAT` reuse proven `zr_aot_f19` directly for `zr_aot_s31 = (TZrInt64)zr_aot_f19` and `zr_aot_u31 = (TZrUInt64)zr_aot_f19`. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. Destination frame writes, generic float copy/type checks, and return/result materialization remain open for later 07-S2 slices.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 f64 stack-copy local-only validation removed the next frame-backed copy shape for float scalar locals. When both source and destination have `f64` C locals, `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_stack_copy_f64()` now emits direct assignments such as `zr_aot_f40 = zr_aot_f19;` and `zr_aot_f22 = zr_aot_f40;` instead of building `SZrTypeValue` source/destination pointers, checking source float tags, releasing destination slots, and writing `ZR_VALUE_TYPE_DOUBLE` frame payloads. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. Non-f64 stack-copy frame writes, scalar result materialization, and return/result frame fallbacks remain open for later 07-S2 slices.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 scalar stack-copy local-only validation extended the same frame-write elimination to bool, signed i64, and unsigned u64 scalar copies. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_stack_copy_bool()`, `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_stack_copy_i64()`, and `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_stack_copy_u64()` now emit direct local assignments when source and destination both have scalar locals, including `zr_aot_b5 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_b7 != 0u);`, `zr_aot_u9 = zr_aot_u12;`, `zr_aot_u21 = zr_aot_u33;`, `zr_aot_s13 = zr_aot_s16;`, and `zr_aot_s18 = zr_aot_s19;`. Those focused copies no longer build source/destination `SZrTypeValue` pointers, perform source tag checks, release destination frame slots, or write destination frame payload fields. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar executable fixture passing with 1 test, the source-contract binary passing with 19 tests, and the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passing. Result materialization, primitive constant frame writes, and return/result frame fallbacks remain open for later 07-S2 slices.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 unsigned compare bool result-local validation extended the result-skip proof from u64 values to bool scalar locals. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_u64_compare()` now calls `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_bool_result_can_skip_value_slot()` after proving both u64 sources are written, so the focused generated C emits only `zr_aot_b14 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_u8 > zr_aot_u7);` and `zr_aot_b23 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_u21 <= zr_aot_u7);` for those compare blocks. The `dstSlot=23` value is consumed directly by `JUMP_IF_BOOL_FALSE`, while the unused `dstSlot=14` value is killed by reset-stack-null; neither compare block builds `SZrTypeValue *zr_aot_destination`, assigns `zr_aot_u_result`, or writes a bool frame payload. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 RESET_STACK_NULL scalar-local validation removed the first single-slot reset frame write from the typed scalar hot path. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_reset_can_skip_value_slot()` now proves a scalar-local reset is dead when all reachable paths overwrite or kill the slot before any source/frame read, and `backend_aot_write_c_reset_stack_null_scalar_local_skip()` emits a marker-only comment instead of the old `SZrTypeValue` destination reset block. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 RESET_STACK_NULL2 scalar-local validation extended that reset proof to paired resets only when both slots are independently dead. `backend_aot_c_function_body.c` skips a reset2 block only if both targets pass `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_reset_can_skip_value_slot()`, and the emitter writes `zr_aot_reset_stack_null2_scalar_local_skip slots=A,B` instead of constructing two `SZrTypeValue` pointers. In that slice the first candidate `slots=3,4` was revised because the proof still treated each slot independently and did not carry paired live state; the accepted focused pair was `slots=5,6`, which is overwritten before any later read. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 RESET_STACK_NULL2 stateful-pair validation removed the remaining focused typed-scalar reset2 frame blocks. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_reset2_can_skip_value_slots()` now tracks first/second reset targets with a live bitmask through the current block suffix and successor graph, allowing the two slots to be overwritten at different instructions before any frame-dependent read. The proof also now asks read predicates only for opcodes that are real scalar-local consumers, so a `GET_CONSTANT` destination is treated as an overwrite rather than a read. Generated typed scalar C now contains reset2 skip markers for `slots=3,4`, `slots=5,6`, `slots=6,7`, `slots=9,10`, and `slots=15,16`, with no `zr_aot_value_exec_reset_stack_null2` block. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S2 i64 direct-return boundary-local validation tightened the previously accepted return-local path. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_return_i64_local()` now reuses the function-scope `zr_aot_call_info` emitted by frame setup instead of redeclaring it from `frame.callInfo` inside the return block, and no longer emits the `frame.function` null guard or constructor-name branch. Generated typed scalar C still writes interpreter-boundary return values directly from `zr_aot_s23` and `zr_aot_s48`, preserves ownership release and closure cleanup, and no longer contains return-local `frame.callInfo`, `frame.function->functionName`, or `zr_aot_result_slot = frame.slotBase + N`. WSL GCC reports the typed scalar fixture passing with 1 test, source contracts passing 19 tests, and return contracts passing 1 test; the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passes while return-contract binaries are not registered as CTest targets in this build. `tests/parser/test_aot_c_typed_scalar.c` is now 1025 lines; this slice kept the existing focused generated-product fixture whole and records the smallest follow-up split as extracting marker/forbidden-token assertions once 07-S2 stabilizes.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S3 frame setup observation validation removed setup-time observation/default-debug initialization from `backend_aot_write_c_frame_setup()`. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S5 return-boundary module validation then split the i64 return marshaling helper out of the monolithic runtime source. `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ReturnI64()` is implemented in `aot_runtime/aot_runtime_return.c`, and `aot_runtime_internal.h` is the narrow private bridge from boundary modules back to runtime state lookup and shared failure reporting. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S5 inline-struct return-boundary validation moved value SemIR typed inline-struct returns through `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ReturnInlineStruct()`. Generated typed return blocks now call the runtime helper with `sourceSlot`, `sourceTypeLayoutId`, byte offset/size, and `&zr_aot_skip_drop_slot`, then return, instead of directly resolving layouts, writing `state->stackTop.valuePointer`, or assigning the skip-drop slot. The same slice materializes typed-call/static-direct VALUE argument source slots before `ZrCore_Function_PreCallPreparedResolvedVmFunctionWithArgumentSource`, tightens scalar stack-copy lowering so whole-function scalar-local declarations cannot make a not-yet-written struct/object temporary read as i64, and makes direct stack-copy fallback use `ZrCore_Function_CopyFrameSlotInline()` for inline-struct source/destination pairs with the same layout. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S5 call inline-struct boundary validation then moved the value SemIR typed inline-struct call boundary into `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallInlineStruct()`. The helper centralizes the current VM call-frame preparation, VALUE argument source materialization, callee thunk invocation, `PostCall`, and caller frame restoration. Generated typed-call blocks now emit a single helper guard carrying destination/callee/argument/layout/thunk data, so the generated C no longer expands the old `SZrCallInfo`, callable `SZrTypeValue`, `ZrCore_Function_PreCallPreparedResolvedVmFunctionWithArgumentSource`, or `ZrCore_Function_PostCall` template in this path. WSL GCC reports the same focused group passing: source contracts 19 tests, return contracts 1 test, frame setup contracts 1 test, typed scalar 1 test, value SemIR contracts 4 tests, call contracts 4 tests, and call shared-library smoke 3 tests; the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passes. This is still a boundary-template consolidation, not the final typed-to-typed native signature ABI.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S5 static direct-call boundary validation moved the ordinary static direct-call VM boundary into `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallStaticDirect()`. The helper owns the current call-frame preparation, VALUE argument source materialization, callee thunk invocation, `PostCall`, and caller frame restoration. Generated static direct-call blocks now retain only the `zr_aot_direct_static_function_call` marker plus one helper guard with destination slot, function slot, argument count, callee index, and callee thunk. The source and smoke contracts reject the old generated `ZrCore_Function_PreCallPreparedResolvedVmFunctionWithArgumentSource`, `zr_aot_materialize_argument_source_slot`, and `ZrCore_Function_PostCall(state, zr_aot_call_info, 1)` sequence in that call block. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S5 call stack-value boundary validation then moved generic/dynamic stack-value function calls into `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallStackValue()`. The helper owns the existing call-base/destination anchors, `ZrCore_Function_CallAndRestoreAnchor`, result slot copy, and caller frame refresh. Generated generic/dynamic call blocks now keep only the existing `zr_aot_direct_function_call` / `zr_aot_direct_dynamic_function_call` marker plus one helper guard. The call contracts reject the old generated `SZrFunctionStackAnchor` and `CallAndRestoreAnchor` template in `backend_aot_c_lowering_calls.c`, and the call smoke rejects it in generated C. WSL GCC reports source contracts passing 19 tests, return contracts 1 test, frame setup contracts 1 test, typed scalar 1 test, value SemIR contracts 4 tests, call contracts 4 tests, and call shared-library smoke 3 tests; the registered `aot_c_typed_scalar` CTest passes. This remains a VM-boundary template consolidation pending typed-to-typed native signature routing.

Focused 2026-06-21 07-S5 unsupported meta-call boundary validation then moved the current unsupported meta-call block into `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_UnsupportedMetaCall()`. Generated meta-call blocks keep only the `zr_aot_unsupported_meta_call` marker plus one helper guard, so the generated C no longer expands destination/receiver/argument locals, `SZrTypeValue *` slot access, or the meta-specific `ZrCore_Debug_RunError(state, "unsupported AOT meta call")` template. The same validation repaired scalar stack-copy proof propagation so an f64 local copy like `22 <- 40` can inherit the source slot's declared scalar kind and remain local-only, preserving the 07-S4 focused typed-scalar frame-free contract. The source-contract suite now also locks legacy int arithmetic direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_legacy_int_arithmetic_to_direct_c_expressions` first failed on missing `zr_aot_arith_exec_int`, then passed after `ADD_INT`, `ADD_INT_CONST`, `SUB_INT`, and `SUB_INT_CONST` moved into `backend_aot_c_lowering_legacy_int_arithmetic.c`. The contract requires the direct stack/stack and stack/constant `+` / `-` expression shapes, the shared integer-like constant literal formatter, function-body routing for both const and non-const int opcodes, explicit unsupported const failures, and absence of generated-C `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_AddIntConst`, `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SubInt`, and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SubIntConst` calls in that lowering module.

The source-contract suite now locks generic numeric arithmetic boundary-helper lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_numeric_arithmetic_to_boundary_helpers` first failed after requiring `zr_aot_arith_exec_generic_numeric_binary_boundary` and the `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericNumeric*()` helper family while the generator still expanded direct tag branches. It passed after generic `ADD`, `SUB`, `MUL`, `DIV`, `MOD`, and `NEG` moved to helper guards and the numeric primitive branches moved into `aot_runtime_values.c`. The contract requires emitter declarations and function-body routing for those opcodes, generated boundary markers and helper calls, runtime helper declarations and implementations, preservation of `divide by zero`, `modulo by zero`, and `fmod(leftFloat, rightFloat)` semantics, and absence of old generated numeric extraction helpers, direct `ZrCore_Stack_GetValue(frame.slotBase + %u)` locals, generated tag ladders, direct expression strings, and generated unary negation templates.

The source-contract suite now also locks generic primitive conversion boundary-helper lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_primitive_conversions_to_boundary_helpers` first failed after requiring helper-only generic primitive conversion lowering, then passed after generic `TO_BOOL`, `TO_INT`, `TO_UINT`, and `TO_FLOAT` moved onto dedicated `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ConvertGenericTo*()` helpers. The contract requires conversion markers and helper guards in generated C, helper declarations and implementations in the AOT runtime, and absence of generated direct conversion stack locals, tag-branch templates, generated unsupported conversion blocks, or broader `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_To*()` helper reuse from the generated lowering path.

The AOT C source-contract suite now has a separate logical contract target so the older source-contract file does not keep growing past its current large-file boundary. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_truthiness_to_boundary_helpers` first failed after requiring helper-only generic primitive truthiness lowering, then passed after generic `LOGICAL_NOT` and `JUMP_IF` moved onto dedicated `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericPrimitiveLogicalNot()` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericPrimitiveIsTruthy()` helpers. The 2026-06-22 local-sync tightening then required `zr_aot_generic_logical_sync_bool_local_boundary` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SyncBoolLocal()` for helper-written bool destinations, forbidding the old generated `zr_aot_bool_sync` slot lookup and payload reload. The contract requires generated markers, helper guards, bool scalar-local sync after helper-written `LOGICAL_NOT` destinations, runtime primitive truthiness helper coverage, and absence of old generated primitive truthiness branch templates or broader `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_LogicalNot` / `IsTruthy` calls from the generic logical lowering path.

The logical source-contract suite now also locks generic primitive equality boundary-helper lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_primitive_equality_to_boundary_helpers` first failed after requiring helper-only generic primitive equality lowering, then passed after generic `LOGICAL_EQUAL` and `LOGICAL_NOT_EQUAL` moved onto dedicated `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericPrimitiveLogicalEqual()` and `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericPrimitiveLogicalNotEqual()` helpers. The 2026-06-22 local-sync tightening also makes equality/inequality bool scalar-local refresh helper-owned via `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SyncBoolLocal()`, so generated C no longer emits `const SZrTypeValue *zr_aot_bool_sync = ZrCore_Stack_GetValue(frame.slotBase + slot)`. The contract requires generated markers, helper guards, bool scalar-local sync after helper-written destinations, runtime primitive equality helper coverage, and absence of old generated same-type/equality branch templates, generated unsupported equality blocks, `ZrCore_Value_Equal`, or broader `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_LogicalEqual` / `LogicalNotEqual` calls from the generic logical lowering path.

The logical source-contract suite now also locks bool binary logical direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_bool_logical_and_or_to_direct_c` first failed on missing `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_and`, then passed after `LOGICAL_AND` and `LOGICAL_OR` were routed through direct generated-C emitters in `backend_aot_c_lowering_generic_logical.c`. The logical source-contract suite now also locks typed string equality direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_string_equality_to_direct_c` first failed on missing `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_equal_string`, then passed after `LOGICAL_EQUAL_STRING` and `LOGICAL_NOT_EQUAL_STRING` were routed through direct generated-C emitters in `backend_aot_c_lowering_generic_logical.c`. The shift source-contract suite now locks generic integer shift direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_integer_shift_to_direct_c` first failed on missing generic shift direct emitter declarations, then passed after generic `SHIFT_LEFT` and `SHIFT_RIGHT` moved from `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ShiftLeft` / `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ShiftRight` helper calls to direct generated-C emitters in `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_bitwise.c`. The float source-contract suite now locks typed float modulo direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_float_mod_to_direct_c` first failed because `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_float_mod.c` did not exist, then passed after `MOD_FLOAT` moved from `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ModFloat(state, &frame, ...)` to a direct generated-C `fmod` emitter. The contract requires the new emitter declaration, generated module `#include <math.h>`, float operand validation, direct `fmod(zr_aot_left_scalar, zr_aot_right_scalar)`, a `modulo by zero` guard, direct `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` result writes, function-body routing for `MOD_FLOAT`, and absence of the old `ModFloat` helper route from the C lowering path.

The generic numeric source-contract suite now locks generic `MOD` float fallback through the same boundary helper. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_generic_numeric_mod_float_fallback_to_boundary_helper` requires generated C to call `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_GenericNumericMod(state, &frame, %u, %u, %u)` while `aot_runtime_values.c` owns `<math.h>`, `modulo by zero`, and `fmod(leftFloat, rightFloat)`. The contract rejects the old generated float branch, shared zero-guard emitter, direct `fmod(zr_aot_left_float, zr_aot_right_float)`, direct `ZR_VALUE_TYPE_DOUBLE` write, and signed/unsigned direct `%` expression templates from the C lowering module.

The power source-contract suite now locks typed power direct lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_power_to_direct_c` first failed because `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_power.c` did not exist, then passed after `POW_SIGNED`, `POW_UNSIGNED`, and `POW_FLOAT` moved from typed power runtime helper calls to direct generated-C emitters. The contract requires direct emitter declarations, signed/unsigned/float operand validation, `power domain error`, integer exponentiation-by-squaring loop markers, direct `pow(zr_aot_left_scalar, zr_aot_right_scalar)`, direct `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` result writes, function-body routing for the three typed opcodes, and absence of the old typed power helper routes from the C lowering path.

The same source-contract suite now also checks signed load-const arithmetic as a separate module boundary. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_load_const_arithmetic_to_c_expressions` first failed because `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_arithmetic_load_const.c` did not exist, then passed after the module was added and `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST`, `SUB_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST`, `MUL_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST`, `DIV_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST`, and `MOD_SIGNED_LOAD_CONST` were routed through direct C emitters. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_load_stack_const_arithmetic_to_c_expressions` first failed on missing stack-const emitter declarations, then passed after the same module added direct lowering for `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`, `SUB_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`, `MUL_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`, `DIV_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`, and `MOD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST`. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_load_stack_load_const_arithmetic_to_c_expressions` first failed on missing `backend_aot_write_c_direct_add_signed_load_stack_load_const`, then passed after `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_LOAD_CONST` was routed through direct materialization and C `+` lowering. `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_load_stack_arithmetic_to_c_expressions` first failed because `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_arithmetic_load_stack.c` was missing, then passed after `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK` was routed through direct stack/stack C `+` lowering; it later failed on missing `zr_aot_left_scalar * zr_aot_right_scalar`, then passed after `MUL_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK` joined the same direct stack/stack lowering module with an `INT64` result tag. The contracts lock constant and stack-source materialization, direct `+`, `-`, `*`, `/`, `%` expressions, divide/modulo zero guards, function-body routing, and executable-subset support for these signed quickening families.

The same test now locks typed signed/unsigned `%` lowering: direct emitter declarations, `zr_aot_left_scalar % zr_aot_right_scalar`, `zr_aot_left_scalar % zr_aot_right_literal`, `ADD_SIGNED_MOD_CONST`'s direct add-plus-mod expression, `modulo by zero`, function-body routing for typed modulo opcodes, and absence of direct signed/unsigned modulo helper strings for those opcode families. It also locks typed numeric comparison lowering: signed/unsigned/float comparison emitter declarations, `zr_aot_compare_exec_*` source markers, `==`, `!=`, `>`, `<`, `>=`, and `<=` scalar expressions, function-body routing for typed numeric comparison opcodes, and absence of direct `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_Logical*` helper strings for those opcode families.

The bitwise source-contract test `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_bitwise_to_c_expressions` locks the separate typed bitwise lowering module, emitter declarations, C expression shapes for `~`, `&`, `|`, `^`, signed shift-right, unsigned left/right shift intermediates, shift-count range checks, function-body routing for typed bitwise and shift opcodes, and absence of direct bitwise/typed-shift runtime helper strings for those opcode families.

The bool logical source-contract test `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_bool_equality_to_c_expressions` locks the separate typed logical lowering module, bool equality and logical-not emitter declarations, `zr_aot_bool_compare_exec` / `zr_aot_bool_not_exec` source markers, direct `==` / `!=` / `!` bool expressions, function-body routing for `LOGICAL_EQUAL_BOOL` / `LOGICAL_NOT_EQUAL_BOOL` / `LOGICAL_NOT_BOOL`, typed bool false-branch routing for `JUMP_IF_BOOL_FALSE`, `zr_aot_jump_if_bool_false`, and absence of direct bool equality/logical-not runtime helper strings for those proven-bool opcode families.

The signed branch source-contract test `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_signed_branch_to_c_comparisons` locks the fused signed branch family. It requires direct emitter declarations for `JUMP_IF_GREATER_SIGNED`, `JUMP_IF_LESS_EQUAL_SIGNED`, `JUMP_IF_NOT_EQUAL_SIGNED`, and `JUMP_IF_NOT_EQUAL_SIGNED_CONST`; direct generated C comparison expressions for `>`, `<=`, slot/slot `!=`, and slot/constant `!=`; function-body routing; executable-subset support; AotExecIR conditional-branch recognition; and absence of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_ShouldJumpIfGreaterSigned` from the C control lowering module.

The focused signed slot/slot branch contract is now guarded by same-basic-block local-written-before proof. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_i64_written_before()` only proves an `sN` local usable when the current basic block contains an earlier write from a SemIR destination, immediate scalar constant, numeric conversion destination, or stack-copy propagation source. With that proof, the generated branch keeps frame-slot bounds and signed-type tag checks but branches directly on `if (zr_aot_sL op zr_aot_sR)` without refreshing `sN` from `zr_aot_left/right->value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` inside the branch. This deliberately does not prove cross-block joins, entry parameters, or resume/deopt restored local state.

The numeric conversion source-contract test `test_aot_c_source_lowers_typed_numeric_conversion_to_c_casts` locks the separate typed conversion lowering module, direct emitter declarations for signed/unsigned-to-float, float-to-signed/unsigned, unsigned-to-signed, and signed-to-unsigned conversion helpers, the `zr_aot_convert_signed_to_float` / `zr_aot_convert_unsigned_to_float` / `zr_aot_convert_float_to_signed` / `zr_aot_convert_unsigned_to_signed` / `zr_aot_convert_float_to_unsigned` / `zr_aot_convert_signed_to_unsigned` source markers, direct `(TZrFloat64)`, `(TZrInt64)`, and `(TZrUInt64)` cast expressions, the `zr_aot_unsigned_to_signed_limit` wrap expression, and function-body routing for `TO_FLOAT_SIGNED` / `TO_FLOAT_UNSIGNED` / `TO_INT_FLOAT` / `TO_INT_UNSIGNED` / `TO_UINT_FLOAT` / `TO_UINT_SIGNED`.

The AOT M2 typed scalar generated-product contract now also locks the first scalar C local mirror path for focused numeric conversions. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals.c` gathers local declarations from typed local bindings, SemIR destination static C types, and focused typed numeric conversion bytecode destinations. Reused conversion temporary slots can therefore declare all proven mirrors, for example `zr_aot_s29`, `zr_aot_u29`, and `zr_aot_f29`; `backend_aot_c_scalar_conversion.c` then writes destination-local casts such as `zr_aot_f29 = (TZrFloat64)zr_aot_s2;`, `zr_aot_s29 = (TZrInt64)zr_aot_f17;`, and `zr_aot_u29 = (TZrUInt64)zr_aot_f17;` before mirroring through the existing result/frame-slot path. This is still a focused scalar subset: generic value-source conversions, non-numeric conversions, broader branch forms, and full C-local/frame-slot coherence remain later AOT plan work.

The scalar destination-local fallback mirror contract now covers arithmetic, compare, bitwise, bit-not, and shift templates whose operands are not all proven local. Those paths still validate/read frame slots into temporary result expressions, but if the destination slot has scalar-local coverage they now mirror the computed `zr_aot_s_result`, `zr_aot_u_result`, `zr_aot_f_result`, or bool compare result into `zr_aot_sN`, `zr_aot_uN`, `zr_aot_fN`, or `zr_aot_bN` before the existing frame-slot write. This keeps destination locals coherent after fallback computations without yet making locals the authoritative source for every operand.

The focused scalar stack-copy generated-product contract now keeps declared scalar source and destination locals coherent for the first bool/i64/u64/f64 copy subset. `backend_aot_c_scalar_stack_copy.c` still validates source and destination frame slots and writes the copied payload through the existing `SZrTypeValue` frame-slot ABI, but when source scalar-local coverage is proven it reads the copy payload from `zr_aot_bN`, `zr_aot_sN`, `zr_aot_uN`, or `zr_aot_fN`, and when destination scalar-local coverage is proven it mirrors the copied value into the destination local. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals.c` also propagates scalar-local kind across `GET_STACK` / `SET_STACK` destinations when the source slot is proven local, so the focused f64 copy chain declares `zr_aot_f40`, writes `zr_aot_f40 = zr_aot_f_value`, then reads `zr_aot_f_value = zr_aot_f40` before mirroring into `zr_aot_f22`. The executable typed-scalar golden locks the bool path with `zr_aot_b_value = zr_aot_b7;` and `zr_aot_b5 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_b_value != 0u);` before the focused `branchFlag` false branch consumes `zr_aot_b5`. This closes only the focused scalar-copy source/destination local mirror and destination-propagation slice; systematic C-local storage ownership and GC-root coherence remain later work.

The same generated-product contract now covers the first signed const branch local predicate. The focused source `if (product == 42)` quickens to `JUMP_IF_NOT_EQUAL_SIGNED_CONST`; generated C must sync the left slot into `zr_aot_s2`, emit `if (zr_aot_s2 != zr_aot_right_literal) {`, and reject the older `if (zr_aot_left_scalar != zr_aot_right_literal) {` predicate in that path. This closes only the focused signed const branch local-predicate slice, not the broader branch matrix.

The bool branch generated-product contract now also covers the focused `branchFlag` false-branch path. Generated C must keep `branchFlag` mirrored into `zr_aot_b5` during the preceding scalar stack-copy, emit the proven-local marker `zr_aot_jump_if_bool_false_scalar_local`, branch with `if (!zr_aot_b5) {`, and reject both the older `if (!zr_aot_condition_bool) {` fallback predicate and the older proven-local refresh `zr_aot_b5 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_condition->value.nativeObject.nativeBool != 0u);`. This closes only the focused straight-line `JUMP_IF_BOOL_FALSE` condition-local predicate slice; resume/deopt entry local-state reconstruction remains later work.

The same bool branch path now uses the shared same-basic-block written-before proof instead of broad bool local declaration coverage. `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_bool_written_before()` reuses the scalar-kind proof used by signed branches and only permits `if (!zr_aot_bN)` when an earlier instruction in the current block wrote the bool local through SemIR, an immediate constant, conversion, or stack-copy propagation. The focused `branchFlag` and unsigned-compare false branches still get the no-refresh generated shape, but unproven bool branches fall back to validating the frame slot and reading `zr_aot_condition_bool`.

The focused unsigned compare branch check confirms there is no independent unsigned/f64 branch lowering entry for `if (unsignedInverted <= unsignedRight)`. That source path lowers to `zr_aot_scalar_exec_u64_compare`, writes `zr_aot_b23 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_u21 <= zr_aot_u7);`, mirrors `zr_aot_u_result = zr_aot_b23;`, and then consumes the bool local through the existing `zr_aot_jump_if_bool_false_scalar_local` path with `if (!zr_aot_b23) {`. Broader branch coverage therefore belongs to the local-state/control-flow matrix, not to a separate unsigned branch helper.

The signed slot/slot branch generated-product contract now rejects the older `zr_aot_s2 = zr_aot_left_scalar;` and `zr_aot_s4 = zr_aot_right_scalar;` synchronization shape. Proven local operands must be copied directly from the validated frame-slot value pointers into `zr_aot_s2` and `zr_aot_s4` before the `sN` predicate. This closes only the focused fused signed slot/slot direct-sync slice.

The signed `i64` binary generated-product contract now also rejects the older `zr_aot_s0 = zr_aot_s_left;` synchronization shape on the first covered `left * right` local-expression path. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[0].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` and `frame.slotBase[1].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s0` and `zr_aot_s1` before emitting `zr_aot_s2 = zr_aot_s0 * zr_aot_s1;`. This is still a focused 04-S3 frame-slot-to-`sN` sync slice rather than full C-local/frame-slot coherence.

The unsigned `u64` binary generated-product contract follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `unsignedLeft + unsignedRight` path. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[6].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` and `frame.slotBase[7].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` into `zr_aot_u6` and `zr_aot_u7` before emitting `zr_aot_u8 = zr_aot_u6 + zr_aot_u7;`, rejecting the older `zr_aot_u6 = zr_aot_u_left;` synchronization shape. This remains a focused scalar subset and does not yet make C locals the authoritative storage for every path.

The `f64` binary generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `floatLeft * floatRight` path. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[17].value.value.nativeObject.nativeDouble` and `frame.slotBase[18].value.value.nativeObject.nativeDouble` into `zr_aot_f17` and `zr_aot_f18` before emitting `zr_aot_f30 = zr_aot_f17 * zr_aot_f18;`, rejecting the older `zr_aot_f17 = zr_aot_f_left;` synchronization shape. This still mirrors results back through frame slots and is not a full C-local storage model.

The signed `i64` binary bitwise generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `masked = maskBase & left` path. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[10].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` and `frame.slotBase[0].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s10` and `zr_aot_s0` before emitting `zr_aot_s14 = zr_aot_s10 & zr_aot_s0;`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_s10 = zr_aot_s_left;` / `zr_aot_s0 = zr_aot_s_right;` synchronization shape for this path. Fallback bitwise lowering can still use local `zr_aot_s_left` / `zr_aot_s_right` temporaries when scalar locals are not proven; shift and bit-not direct-sync coverage remain separate slices.

The signed `i64` shift generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `shifted = toggled << right` and `shiftedBack = shifted >> right` paths. Proven local operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[13].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` / `frame.slotBase[14].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` and `frame.slotBase[1].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s13` / `zr_aot_s14` and `zr_aot_s1`, then check `zr_aot_s1` for the signed shift-count range before emitting `zr_aot_s17 = (TZrInt64)((TZrUInt64)zr_aot_s13 << zr_aot_s1);` or `zr_aot_s18 = zr_aot_s14 >> zr_aot_s1;`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_s13 = zr_aot_s_left;`, `zr_aot_s14 = zr_aot_s_left;`, and `zr_aot_s1 = zr_aot_s_shift;` synchronization shape for these paths. Fallback shift lowering can still use local `zr_aot_s_left` / `zr_aot_s_shift` temporaries when scalar operands are not proven.

The signed `i64` bit-not generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `inverted = ~right` path. Proven local source operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[1].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s1` before emitting `zr_aot_s17 = ~zr_aot_s1;`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_s1 = zr_aot_s_source;` synchronization shape for this path. Fallback bit-not lowering can still use local `zr_aot_s_source` when the source scalar local is not proven.

The unsigned `u64` binary bitwise generated-product contract now has the same direct-sync module boundary as signed `i64` bitwise. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_u64_bitwise()` receives the current `SZrAotExecIrFunction`, checks destination/left/right with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_u64_slot`, and on the proven-local path emits direct `frame.slotBase[8]` / `frame.slotBase[7]` unsigned loads into `zr_aot_u8` / `zr_aot_u7` before `zr_aot_u12 = zr_aot_u8 & zr_aot_u7;` for the focused `unsignedMasked = unsignedSum & unsignedRight` path. The fallback path can still use `zr_aot_u_left` / `zr_aot_u_right` temporaries when scalar locals are not proven. The executable typed-scalar golden now covers this path after the interpreter generic unsigned bitwise result type was fixed to preserve `ZR_VALUE_TYPE_UINT64` for unsigned operands.

The unsigned `u64` bit-not generated-product contract now follows the same boundary. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_u64_bit_not()` receives `SZrAotExecIrFunction`, checks source/destination with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_u64_slot`, and on the proven-local path emits a direct `frame.slotBase[7].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` load into `zr_aot_u7` before `zr_aot_u33 = ~zr_aot_u7;` for the focused `unsignedInverted = ~unsignedRight` path after the unsigned shift temporaries. The fallback path still uses `zr_aot_u_source` when the source local is not proven. The executable typed-scalar golden now covers this path, rejects the old `ZrCore_Stack_GetValue` / `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` route, and keeps the result mirrored through the existing frame slot ABI.

The unsigned `u64` shift generated-product contract now runs end to end in the focused typed-scalar executable. `compile_expression.c` preserves the original typed operands for `<<` / `>>` instead of converting the signed shift count to the unsigned result type, and selects `BITWISE_SHIFT_LEFT` / `BITWISE_SHIFT_RIGHT` when the effective typed operands include an unsigned integer. `backend_aot_write_c_scalar_u64_shift()` checks the left operand with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_u64_slot`, checks the signed shift-count operand with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_i64_slot`, checks the destination with `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_has_u64_slot`, and on the proven-local path emits direct `frame.slotBase` loads into `zr_aot_uN` / `zr_aot_sN`. The focused generated product now covers `unsignedShifted = unsignedSum << right` and `unsignedShiftedBack = unsignedShifted >> right`, emitting `zr_aot_scalar_exec_u64_shift`, `zr_aot_u13 = zr_aot_u8 << zr_aot_s1;`, and `zr_aot_u14 = zr_aot_u10 >> zr_aot_s1;` while keeping the forbidden `ZrCore_Stack_GetValue` / `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` scan at zero. Fallback shift lowering keeps `zr_aot_u_left` / `zr_aot_s_shift` temporaries for unproven operands.

The signed `i64` scalar compare generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `product > threshold` path. Proven compare operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[2].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` and `frame.slotBase[4].value.value.nativeObject.nativeInt64` into `zr_aot_s2` and `zr_aot_s4` before emitting `zr_aot_b25 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_s2 > zr_aot_s4);`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_s2 = zr_aot_s_left;` / `zr_aot_s4 = zr_aot_s_right;` synchronization shape for this path. Fallback compare lowering can still use local `zr_aot_s_left` / `zr_aot_s_right` temporaries when scalar locals are not proven.

The unsigned `u64` scalar compare generated-product contract now follows the same direct-sync rule for the first covered `unsignedSum > unsignedRight` path. Proven compare operands must be copied directly from `frame.slotBase[8].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` and `frame.slotBase[7].value.value.nativeObject.nativeUInt64` into `zr_aot_u8` and `zr_aot_u7` before emitting `zr_aot_b12 = (TZrBool)(zr_aot_u8 > zr_aot_u7);`. The generated product rejects the older `zr_aot_u8 = zr_aot_u_left;` / `zr_aot_u7 = zr_aot_u_right;` synchronization shape for this path. Fallback compare lowering can still use local `zr_aot_u_left` / `zr_aot_u_right` temporaries when scalar operands are not proven.

The scalar SemIR dispatcher now keeps binary arithmetic in a separate module boundary. `backend_aot_c_scalar_semir.c` remains the small dispatcher and comparison lowering surface: it handles scalar conversion, bitwise, binary, unsigned compare, and signed compare in that order. The signed `i64`, unsigned `u64`, and `f64` binary arithmetic emitters, operand decoders, direct frame-slot-to-`sN` / `uN` / `fN` sync logic, divide/modulo guards, and plain scalar result writers live in `backend_aot_c_scalar_binary.{h,c}`. The source-contract test reads both the dispatcher and binary module, so future binary arithmetic changes should land in the binary module instead of growing the dispatcher again.

`backend_aot_c_value_semir.c` is verified with constrained GCC/Clang syntax checks because the archived AOT backend is not in the active CMake target graph. The focused AOT C syntax checks now cover the frame cleanup, function body, value SemIR, control lowering, values lowering, legacy int arithmetic, typed arithmetic, load-const arithmetic, load-stack arithmetic, and backend gating sources with the public include paths and public `SZrAotWriterOptions` declaration, so the source-contract test is backed by direct compiler coverage for the touched AOT C emitters.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 bool binary logical opcode scalar-local validation applies the same local-only rule to `LOGICAL_AND` and `LOGICAL_OR` bytecode lowering. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_and()` and `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_or()` now receive the instruction index, use bool result-skip and left/right written-before proofs, and emit `zr_aot_bool_binary_scalar_local` with a direct `zr_aot_bN` assignment when the proof holds. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 string equality bool-result scalar-local validation removes the destination value-slot write from proven string equality bool results. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_equal_string()` and `backend_aot_write_c_direct_logical_not_equal_string()` now receive the instruction index and can emit `zr_aot_string_logical_bool_scalar_local` when the bool destination can skip its value slot. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 typed power scalar-local validation removes destination value-slot writes from proven typed power results. `backend_aot_write_c_direct_pow_signed()`, `backend_aot_write_c_direct_pow_unsigned()`, and `backend_aot_write_c_direct_pow_float()` now receive the function IR and instruction index, consult result-skip and operand written-before proofs, and emit `zr_aot_arith_exec_*_power_scalar_local` direct assignments to `zr_aot_sN`, `zr_aot_uN`, or `zr_aot_fN` when safe. Unproven paths keep the old frame/value fallback. Scalar-local analysis records non-tail call opcodes as result writes and back-propagates a stack-copy destination kind only when the source slot is a call-result destination; this targeted rule fixes no-arg `uint`/`float` static callees copied into typed locals without reintroducing the broad copy propagation that incorrectly scalarized inline-struct value-type slots. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 MethodInfo signature descriptor validation replaces the old null signature placeholder with a generated per-function descriptor. The public AOT ABI now defines `SZrAotSignatureType` and `SZrAotSignature`; `backend_aot_c_emitter.c` emits `zr_aot_signature_N_types` and `zr_aot_signature_N` from each function's typed return/parameter metadata and stores `&zr_aot_signature_N` in `SZrAotMethodInfo.signature`. The value typed-call shared-library smoke locks the generated shape for a one-parameter callee, including `parameterCount`, non-null `returnType`, and non-null `parameterTypes`. This is the signature metadata source required by later typed-to-typed native C signature routing; it does not yet replace current helper-based static direct calls or inline-struct call/return boundaries with direct typed C call/return lowering. Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 MethodInfo table publication validation makes the generated signature descriptors reachable from the public compiled-module descriptor. The AOT ABI is now version 3 and `ZrAotCompiledModule` exposes `methodInfos` plus `methodInfoCount`; `backend_aot_c_emitter.c` emits a `zr_aot_method_infos[]` table that points at every generated `zr_aot_method_info_N`, then publishes that table and the function count in `zr_aot_compiled_module`. The shared-library smoke loads the generated module and verifies that `module->methodInfos[0]->signature` is non-null. This still remains metadata publication only: typed-to-typed direct C call/return lowering, `in` / `out` writeback, and deopt/dynamic bridge boxing templates remain separate 07-S5 follow-up work. WSL GCC validation reports frame setup contracts 1/0, source contracts 19/0, shared-library smoke 8/0, and the broader focused AOT group passing call, shared-library, value-type, power, source, generic numeric, global, logical, typed-scalar, return, and frame-setup binaries.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static no-arg i64 typed thunk direct-call validation adds the first typed-to-typed direct C call slice. The C emitter recognizes typed no-argument functions with int64 return metadata whose body is a constant signed-int return and emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N` forward declarations and definitions returning `TZrInt64`. Function-body call lowering routes eligible static no-arg i64 call destinations directly through that thunk, assigns the scalar local, and then syncs the destination stack slot with `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` so still-frame-backed later consumers remain correct until the wider 07 cleanup removes them. The dedicated shared-library smoke executes `answer(): int { return 42; }` through the direct path, verifies the typed thunk markers, and rejects generated `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallStaticDirect` / `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallStackValue` in that path. This is intentionally narrow: typed parameter ABI, general returns, inline structs, `in` / `out` writeback, and deopt/dynamic bridge boxing remain follow-up 07-S5 work. WSL GCC validation reports call contracts 5/0, typed direct-call shared-library smoke 1/0, and aggregate shared-library smoke 8/0.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static one-arg i64 typed thunk direct-call validation extends the typed-to-typed path with the first direct C parameter ABI slice. The C emitter recognizes single-parameter typed i64 functions whose body returns parameter slot 0 and emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N(struct SZrState *state, TZrInt64 zr_aot_arg0)`, returning the C argument directly. Function-body call lowering proves the call window's first argument slot (`functionSlot + 1`) is an initialized i64 scalar local before the call and emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N(state, zr_aot_sArg)` instead of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_CallStaticDirect`. The destination still syncs its stack slot with `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET` for current frame-backed consumers. The dedicated shared-library smoke now executes `echo(value: int): int { return value; }` through this route and rejects generated `CallStaticDirect` / `CallStackValue` for the direct typed path. This remains a narrow one-arg identity-return foothold; multi-arg calls, non-identity/general typed returns, inline structs, `in` / `out` writeback, deopt/dynamic bridge boxing, and stack-sync removal remain later 07-S5 work. WSL GCC validation reports call contracts 5/0, typed direct-call shared-library smoke 2/0, and the broader focused AOT group passing call, shared-library, value-type, power, source, generic numeric, global, logical, typed-scalar, return, and frame-setup binaries.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static i64 typed direct-call stack-sync elision validation removes that temporary destination stack-slot sync for the existing no-arg and one-arg direct-thunk routes when scalar-local liveness proves it is unnecessary. The typed direct-call writers now receive `syncStackSlot`; function-body routing computes it from `backend_aot_c_scalar_locals_i64_result_can_skip_value_slot(functionIr, destinationSlot, instructionIndex)`. When later reachable consumers can read `zr_aot_sN`, generated C keeps only the direct C call assignment and omits `SZrTypeValue *zr_aot_typed_destination`, `zr_aot_static_i64_*_direct_call_sync_stack_slot`, and typed-destination `ZR_VALUE_FAST_SET`. The fallback path still writes the stack slot for frame-backed consumers, so this is not a global removal. WSL GCC validation reports call contracts 5/0, typed direct-call shared-library smoke 2/0, and the broader focused AOT group passing call, shared-library, value-type, power, source, generic numeric, global, logical, typed-scalar, return, and frame-setup binaries.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static one-arg i64 arg+constant typed thunk validation broadens the first direct C parameter ABI foothold from identity returns to `return arg0 + signed-constant`. The emitter recognizes both older bytecode add-constant shapes and the SemIR scalar binary form generated as `ADD_SIGNED_LOAD_STACK_CONST` followed by `FUNCTION_RETURN`, then emits `zr_aot_typed_i64_fn_N(struct SZrState *state, TZrInt64 zr_aot_arg0)` with a direct `(TZrInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 + (TZrInt64)K)` return. The dedicated shared-library smoke executes `inc(value: int): int { return value + 1; }` through the one-arg typed direct-call path, verifies runtime result `42`, rejects `CallStaticDirect` / `CallStackValue`, and keeps the scalar-only destination free of typed-destination stack sync. WSL GCC validation reports call contracts 5/0, typed direct-call shared-library smoke 3/0, and the broader focused AOT group passing call, shared-library, value-type, power, source, generic numeric, global, logical, typed-scalar, return, and frame-setup binaries.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static two-arg i64 typed thunk validation adds the next narrow typed parameter ABI slice. This remains narrow u64 bitwise-and coverage and does not close 07-S5.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static two-arg u64 bitwise-or typed thunk validation extends the same unsigned two-parameter route to `return arg0 | arg1`. `backend_aot_c_typed_u64_thunk_shapes.c` now also recognizes `BITWISE_OR` followed by `FUNCTION_RETURN` for two-unsigned-parameter callees, again accepting the parameter operands in either order. `backend_aot_c_typed_u64_thunks.c` includes the OR recognizer in the two-arg u64 can-emit gate and emits the same two-argument thunk signature returning `(TZrUInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 | zr_aot_arg1)`. The u64 shared-library smoke now executes `combine(left: uint, right: uint): uint { return left | right; }` with `40 | 2`, verifies runtime result 42, and rejects the VM call/value fallback path. WSL GCC validation reports typed call contracts 4/0, u64 typed direct-call smoke 10/0, and the broader focused AOT group passing with u64 smoke 10/0. This remains narrow u64 bitwise-or coverage and does not close 07-S5.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static two-arg u64 bitwise-xor typed thunk validation completes the current narrow unsigned two-parameter bitwise trio with `return arg0 ^ arg1`. `backend_aot_c_typed_u64_thunk_shapes.c` now recognizes `BITWISE_XOR` followed by `FUNCTION_RETURN` for the same two-unsigned-parameter callee shape, and the AND/OR/XOR wrappers share a private `backend_aot_c_try_get_u64_arg0_arg1_bitwise_return()` helper for operand/result validation. `backend_aot_c_typed_u64_thunks.c` includes XOR in the two-arg u64 can-emit gate and emits `(TZrUInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 ^ zr_aot_arg1)`. The u64 shared-library smoke now executes `toggle(left: uint, right: uint): uint { return left ^ right; }` with `63 ^ 21`, verifies runtime result 42, and rejects the VM call/value fallback path. WSL GCC validation reports typed call contracts 4/0, u64 typed direct-call smoke 11/0, and the broader focused AOT group passing with u64 smoke 11/0. This covers narrow u64 add/subtract/multiply/AND/OR/XOR two-arg returns, but runtime-failure-capable division/modulo and wider 07-S5 ABI work remain open.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static one-arg u64 bitwise-and-constant typed thunk validation broadens the unsigned one-parameter route from add/subtract/multiply constants to `return arg0 & K`. `backend_aot_c_typed_u64_thunks.c` now recognizes the current SemIR shape generated for `value & 58`: a parameter stack copy, `GET_CONSTANT`, `TO_UINT`, `BITWISE_AND`, and `FUNCTION_RETURN` of the bitwise result. It emits the existing one-argument u64 thunk ABI, returning `(TZrUInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 & (TZrUInt64)K)`, and the direct-call route reuses the scalar-local argument proof and destination sync elision. The u64 shared-library smoke executes `mask(value: uint): uint { return value & 58; }` with seed `47`, verifies runtime result 42, and rejects `CallStaticDirect`, `CallStackValue`, and typed-destination stack sync. Validation first failed on the missing recognizer contract, then failed on the smoke until the `TO_UINT` constant-conversion shape was covered; final WSL GCC validation reports typed call contracts 4/0, u64 typed direct-call smoke 12/0, and the broader focused AOT group passing with u64 smoke 12/0. This remains narrow u64 bitwise-and-constant coverage; one-arg OR/XOR constants and broader 07-S5 ABI work remain open.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static one-arg u64 bitwise-or-constant typed thunk validation extends the same unsigned one-parameter bitwise-constant route to `return arg0 | K`. `backend_aot_c_typed_u64_thunks.c` reuses the private bitwise-constant recognizer and adds a `BITWISE_OR` wrapper, can-emit gate, and writer branch for the existing one-argument `TZrUInt64` thunk ABI. The emitted thunk returns `(TZrUInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 | (TZrUInt64)K)`, and the direct-call route keeps the scalar-local argument proof plus destination sync elision. The u64 shared-library smoke executes `flags(value: uint): uint { return value | 10; }` with seed `32`, verifies runtime result 42, and rejects `CallStaticDirect`, `CallStackValue`, and typed-destination stack sync. WSL GCC validation first failed on the missing OR-constant recognizer contract; after implementation, typed call contracts pass 4/0, u64 typed direct-call smoke passes 13/0, and the broader focused AOT group remains passing with u64 smoke 13/0. This remains narrow u64 bitwise-or-constant coverage; one-arg XOR constants and broader 07-S5 ABI work remain open.

Focused 2026-06-22 07-S5 static one-arg u64 bitwise-xor-constant typed thunk validation completes the current unsigned one-parameter bitwise-constant trio with `return arg0 ^ K`. `backend_aot_c_typed_u64_thunks.c` adds a `BITWISE_XOR` wrapper over the private bitwise-constant recognizer, includes it in the one-arg u64 can-emit gate, and emits a direct `(TZrUInt64)(zr_aot_arg0 ^ (TZrUInt64)K)` return from the existing one-argument thunk ABI. The u64 shared-library smoke executes `toggle(value: uint): uint { return value ^ 21; }` with seed `63`, verifies runtime result 42, and rejects `CallStaticDirect`, `CallStackValue`, and typed-destination stack sync. WSL GCC validation first failed on the missing XOR-constant recognizer contract; after implementation, typed call contracts pass 4/0, u64 typed direct-call smoke passes 14/0, and the broader focused AOT group remains passing with u64 smoke 14/0. This covers narrow u64 one-arg add/subtract/multiply and AND/OR/XOR constant returns, but runtime-failure-capable division/modulo routes and broader 07-S5 ABI work remain open.

Focused 2026-06-06 pending-control direct-core validation originally routed `SET_PENDING_RETURN`, `SET_PENDING_BREAK`, and `SET_PENDING_CONTINUE` through generated direct pending-control blocks and rejected the `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SetPending*` helper route. Focused 2026-06-21 07-S5 pending-control boundary-helper validation supersedes that generated-C shape: `backend_aot_write_c_set_pending_return()`, `backend_aot_write_c_set_pending_break()`, and `backend_aot_write_c_set_pending_continue()` now emit only the existing `zr_aot_pending_*` marker, initialize `zr_aot_next_instruction`, call `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_SetPendingReturn/Break/Continue(..., &zr_aot_next_instruction)`, and dispatch when the helper returns a resume instruction. The runtime helpers own pending-value lookup, pending-control setup, outer-finally resume, target jump, cleanup, frame refresh, and resume-index calculation. WSL GCC focused validation reports source contracts passing with 19 tests, aggregate shared-library smoke passing with 8 tests, and the broader focused AOT group passing source, return, frame setup, typed scalar, value SemIR, call, control, and global contract/smoke binaries. The generated pending-control fixture now contains all three `SetPending*` helper guards and no generated `SZrTypeValue *zr_aot_pending_value`, `execution_set_pending_control`, `execution_resume_pending_via_outer_finally`, `execution_jump_to_instruction_offset`, or `state->pendingControl.targetInstructionOffset` template.

Focused 2026-06-06 TRY/END_TRY direct-core validation extended `tests/parser/test_aot_c_source_contracts.c` and added `tests/parser/test_aot_c_control_shared_library_smoke.c`, registering `zr_vm_aot_c_control_shared_library_smoke_test`. `test_aot_c_source_emits_value_frame_cleanup_exit` first failed on missing `zr_aot_try_direct`, then passed after generated C routed `TRY` and `END_TRY` through direct exception-handler stack operations instead of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_Try` or `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_EndTry`. The focused control smoke hand-builds a minimal `TRY` / `END_TRY` / `FUNCTION_RETURN` function, checks generated direct-control markers and helper absence, and compiles generated C under the Unix toolchain path without executing the exception fixture. GCC and Clang both report the source contract passing with 17 tests and the control shared-library smoke passing with 1 test; MSVC reports the source contract passing with 17 tests and the control smoke target built with its 1 Unix-only runtime check ignored as expected. A production scan over `backend_aot_c*.c` found only `zr_aot_try_direct` / `zr_aot_end_try_direct` marker emission and no `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_Try` or `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_EndTry`. The oversized `tests/parser/test_aot_c_shared_library_smoke.c` remains at 1061 lines; this slice used a new 165-line control smoke instead of growing it further.

Focused 2026-06-06 END_FINALLY direct-core validation added `tests/parser/test_aot_c_control_contracts.c`, updated `tests/parser/test_aot_c_control_shared_library_smoke.c`, and registered `zr_vm_aot_c_control_contracts_test`. The RED source contract first failed on missing `zr_aot_end_finally_direct`; after the implementation, generated C routes `END_FINALLY` through direct handler pop, pending exception unwind, pending return/break/continue resume, pending return-value copy, pending-control cleanup, frame refresh, and generated switch dispatch instead of `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_EndFinally`. GCC and Clang both report `zr_vm_aot_c_source_contracts_test` passing with 17 tests, `zr_vm_aot_c_control_contracts_test` passing with 1 test, and `zr_vm_aot_c_control_shared_library_smoke_test` passing with 1 test. MSVC reports the same source and control contracts passing, and the control smoke target built with its 1 Unix-only runtime check ignored as expected. A production scan over `backend_aot_c*.c` found only the direct exception-control markers and no `ZrLibrary_AotRuntime_Try`, `EndTry`, `Throw`, `Catch`, or `EndFinally` emission. The new control contract keeps END_FINALLY shape assertions out of the already oversized aggregate source-contract file.

Focused 2026-06-04 typed numeric unary validation added `tests/parser/test_typed_numeric_neg.c` and registered `zr_vm_typed_numeric_neg_test`. The signed case compiles `-i` for a statically `int` source, verifies `NEG_SIGNED` is emitted without generic `NEG`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns `-7`. The float case compiles `-f` for a statically `float` source, verifies `NEG_FLOAT` is emitted without generic `NEG`, executes the opcode, and returns a float `-2.0`. The AOT C source contract now also requires `backend_aot_write_c_direct_neg_signed`, `backend_aot_write_c_direct_neg_float`, `zr_aot_arith_exec_signed_unary`, `zr_aot_arith_exec_float_unary`, and `-zr_aot_source_scalar`.

Focused 2026-06-04 typed numeric conversion validation added `tests/parser/test_typed_numeric_conversion.c` and registered `zr_vm_typed_numeric_conversion_test`. The signed-to-float case compiles `return <float> i` for a statically `int` source, verifies `TO_FLOAT_SIGNED` is emitted without generic `TO_FLOAT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns float `7.0`. The unsigned-to-float case compiles `return <float> u` for a statically `uint` source, verifies `TO_FLOAT_UNSIGNED` is emitted without generic `TO_FLOAT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns float `9.0`. The float-to-signed case compiles `return <int> f` for a statically `float` source, verifies `TO_INT_FLOAT` is emitted without generic `TO_INT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns integer `2`. The unsigned-to-signed case compiles `return <int> u` for a statically `uint` source, verifies `TO_INT_UNSIGNED` is emitted without generic `TO_INT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns integer `17`; a high-bit boundary case materializes `<uint>-1`, converts it back through `TO_INT_UNSIGNED`, and returns `-1` with C# unchecked-style wrap semantics. The float-to-unsigned case compiles `return <uint> f` for a statically `float` source, verifies `TO_UINT_FLOAT` is emitted without generic `TO_UINT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns unsigned integer `12`. The signed-to-unsigned case compiles `return <uint> i` for a statically negative `int` source, verifies `TO_UINT_SIGNED` is emitted without generic `TO_UINT`, executes through generated-frame slots, and returns the modulo unsigned payload. The AOT C source contract now also requires `backend_aot_c_lowering_typed_conversion.c`, direct function-body routing, explicit C cast expressions, and the deterministic unsigned-to-signed wrap formula for those six proven numeric conversion forms.

Focused 2026-06-03 validation for the POD return, typed call/return SemIR, first M5 AOT expression-contract slice, executable inline-copy lowering, primitive field load/store lowering, and first typed call/return executable lowering slice passed on WSL GCC and WSL Clang for `zr_vm_semir_pipeline_test`, `zr_vm_instruction_execution_test`, `zr_vm_compiler_integration_test`, and `zr_vm_value_type_runtime_test`. The archived `backend_aot_c_value_semir.c` source also passed GCC and Clang `-fsyntax-only` checks with the required active and archived include roots plus the archived `SZrAotWriterOptions` stub. The same slice also passed an MSVC CLI smoke build and `hello_world.zrp` execution.
